You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// failure case
package xxx;
public class Foo {
    public void bar() {
        String x;
        x = "foo";
        x += "bar";
        x += "baz";
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 2

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Map<String, Integer> variableAppendCounts;

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class);
        variableAppendCounts = new HashMap<String, Integer>();
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        variableAppendCounts.clear();
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() > 0 && node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            String varName = ((ASTVariableAccess) node.jjtGetChild(0)).getImage();
            if (node.getImage().contains("+=")) {
                Integer count = variableAppendCounts.get(varName);
                if (count == null) {
                    count = 0;
                }
                variableAppendCounts.put(varName, ++count);
                if (count > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node, varName);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    private Map<String, Integer> variableAppends;

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class);
        variableAppends = new HashMap<>();
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        variableAppends.clear();
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        variableAppends.clear();
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        if(node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
            ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = (ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            if(assignmentExpression.jjtGetChild(0).getImage() != null) {
                String variableName = assignmentExpression.jjtGetChild(0).getImage();
                Integer count = variableAppends.get(variableName);
                if(count == null) {
                    variableAppends.put(variableName, 1);
                } else {
                    variableAppends.put(variableName, count + 1);
                    if(count >= 2) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(final ASTAssignmentExpression node, final Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 2 && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (varAccess.getType() == String.class && node.getOperator() == ASTAssignmentExpression.Operator.ADD_ASSIGN) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private final Map<String, Integer> variableUseCount = new HashMap<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTName && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTName.class)) {
            ASTName varNameNode = (ASTName) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            String varName = varNameNode.getImage();
            if (node.isAdditive()) {
                variableUseCount.put(varName, variableUseCount.getOrDefault(varName, 0) + 1);
            }
            if(variableUseCount.get(varName) > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public void start(Node node, Object data) {
        variableUseCount.clear();
        super.start(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        Node firstChild = node.jjtGetChild(0);
        if (firstChild instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
            if (parent instanceof ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// compound append, should only report 1 failure
public class Foo {
    public void bar() {
        String x;
        x = "foo";
        x += "bar" + x;
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 2
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        // Checking if the operator is += 
        if (node.isAdditive()) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
            if (parent instanceof ASTAdditiveExpression) {
                ASTAdditiveExpression expr = (ASTAdditiveExpression) parent;
                if (expr.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTName && expr.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTName) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTExpressionStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        Node assignmentOperatorNode = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class); 

        if (assignmentOperatorNode != null && assignmentOperatorNode.getImage().equals("+=")) {
            String variableType = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTVariableDeclaration.class).getTypeImage(); 
            if (variableType.equals("String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTBlock.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        int stringAppendsCount = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(i) instanceof ASTMethodDeclaration) {
                ASTMethodDeclaration methodDeclaration = (ASTMethodDeclaration) node.jjtGetChild(i);
                for (int j = 0; j < methodDeclaration.jjtGetNumChildren(); j++) {
                    if (methodDeclaration.jjtGetChild(j) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator) {
                        ASTAssignmentOperator assignmentOperator = (ASTAssignmentOperator) methodDeclaration.jjtGetChild(j);
                        if (assignmentOperator.isCompound()) {
                            stringAppendsCount++;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        if (stringAppendsCount > 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Set<String> variables = new HashSet<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null) {
                String varName = variableAccess.getVariableName();
                if (variables.contains(varName)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                } else {
                    variables.add(varName);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTExpressionStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        Node assignmentExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null) {
            if (assignmentExpression.hasImageEqualTo("+=")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        Node firstChild = node.jjtGetChild(0);

        if (firstChild instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            String varName = ((ASTVariableAccess) firstChild).getImage();

            if (varName != null && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)) {
                if (node.jjtGetChild(0).getImage().equals(varName)
                        && node.jjtGetChild(1).getImage().startsWith("\"")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Map<String, Integer> variables = new HashMap<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        variables.clear();
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTLocalVariableDeclaration node, Object data) {
        ASTVariableDeclaratorId var = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class);
        if (var != null) {
            variables.put(var.getImage(), 0);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.isCompound()) {
            Node target = assignmentExpression.jjtGetChild(0);
            if (variables.containsKey(target.getImage())) {
                int count = variables.get(target.getImage());
                variables.put(target.getImage(), count + 1);
                if (count >= 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Map<String, Integer> stringVariables = new HashMap<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTBlock.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            AbstractNode child = (AbstractNode) node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTExpressionStatement) {
                ASTExpressionStatement expressionStatement = (ASTExpressionStatement) child;
                ASTAssignmentOperator assignmentOperator = expressionStatement.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
                if (assignmentOperator != null && assignmentOperator.isCompound()) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = expressionStatement.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null) {
                        String variableName = variableAccess.getImage();
                        if (stringVariables.containsKey(variableName)) {
                            stringVariables.put(variableName, stringVariables.get(variableName) + 1);
                            if (stringVariables.get(variableName) > 1) {
                                addViolation(data, variableAccess);
                            }
                        } else {
                            stringVariables.put(variableName, 1);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTLocalVariableDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTLocalVariableDeclaration node, Object data) {
        String varName = ((ASTVariableDeclaratorId) node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class)).getImage();
        ASTBlockStatement block = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTBlockStatement.class);
        int appendCount = 0;
        for (ASTExpressionStatement expr : block.findDescendantsOfType(ASTExpressionStatement.class)) {
            if (expr.hasDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class)) {
                ASTAssignmentOperator assignOp = expr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
                if (assignOp.isCompound()) {
                    ASTVariableDeclaratorId varId = expr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class);
                    if (varId != null && varId.hasImageEqualTo(varName)) {
                        appendCount++;
                        if (appendCount > 1) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
            if (parent instanceof ASTVariableDeclaratorId && TypeHelper.isA((ASTVariableDeclaratorId) parent, String.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTExpressionStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 1 && node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator) {
            ASTAssignmentOperator assignmentOperator = (ASTAssignmentOperator) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            if (assignmentOperator.isCompound()) {
                Node parent = assignmentOperator.jjtGetParent();
                if (parent.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTName) {
                    ASTName name = (ASTName) parent.jjtGetChild(0);
                    if (name.getType() == String.class) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

            addViolation(data, node);

        return super.visit(node, data);

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Map<String, Integer> variables = new HashMap<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTInitializer.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        variables.clear();
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetParent().jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTBlock) {
            String varName = node.jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetChild(0).getImage();
            Integer count = variables.getOrDefault(varName, 0);

            if (node.isCompound()) {
                count++;
                if (count > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            } else {
                count = 0;
            }

            variables.put(varName, count);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    private Map<String, Integer> appendCounts;

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTBlock.class);
        appendCounts = new HashMap<>();
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        appendCounts.clear(); // Clear the counts for each block
        super.visit(node, data);

        for (Integer count : appendCounts.values()) {
            if (count > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
                break;
            }
        }

        return data;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class) != null) {
            String variableName = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class).jjtGetChild(0).getImage();
            appendCounts.put(variableName, appendCounts.getOrDefault(variableName, 0) + 1);
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTBlock.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        int count = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                for (int j = 0; j < child.jjtGetNumChildren(); j++) {
                    Node grandChild = child.jjtGetChild(j);
                    if (grandChild instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator) {
                        count++;
                        if (count > 1) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                            return data;
                        }
                    }
                }
                count = 0;
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        int count = node.jjtGetNumChildren();
        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(i) instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                visit((ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetChild(i), data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        int count = node.jjtGetNumChildren();
        for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(i) instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                visit((ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetChild(i), data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator().equals("+=")) {
            ASTName variable = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTName.class);
            if (variable != null && variable.getType() == String.class) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTBlock.class).stream()
                .flatMap(block -> block.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class).stream())
                .filter(this::isStringAppend)
                .forEach(assignment -> addViolation(data, assignment));
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringAppend(Node node) {
        if (node instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) node;
            if (infixExpression.isAdditive()) {
                return infixExpression.findDescendantsOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).stream()
                        .map(ASTVariableAccess::getVariableNameDeclaration)
                        .filter(Objects::nonNull)
                        .map(VariableNameDeclaration::getType)
                        .anyMatch(type -> type.equals(String.class));
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        Node blockNode = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if(blockNode != null){
            int assignmentCount = blockNode.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class).size();
            if(assignmentCount > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTBlock.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
        if (parent instanceof ASTBlock) {
            Node grandParent = parent.jjtGetParent();
            if (grandParent instanceof ASTMethodDeclaration) {
                ASTMethodDeclaration methodDeclaration = (ASTMethodDeclaration) grandParent;
                if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        Node block = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        int assignmentCounter = block.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class).size();
        if (assignmentCounter > 1) {
            Node localVar = block.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTLocalVariableDeclaration.class);
            String varType = localVar.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTClassOrInterfaceType.class).getTypeImage();
            if ("String".equals(varType)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        checkForStringAppend(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        checkForStringAppend(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkForStringAppend(AbstractJavaNode node, Object data) {
        int numChildren = node.jjtGetNumChildren();
        for (int i = 0; i < numChildren; ++i) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(i) instanceof ASTBlockStatement) {
                ASTBlockStatement blockStatement = (ASTBlockStatement) node.jjtGetChild(i);
                if (blockStatement.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator) {
                    ASTAssignmentOperator operator = (ASTAssignmentOperator) blockStatement.jjtGetChild(0);
                    if (operator.isCompound()) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super("ASTForeachStatement");
        super("ASTWhileStatement");
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        processNode(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        processNode(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void processNode(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(i) instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = (ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetChild(i);
                if (assignmentExpression.getOperator().equals("+=")) {
                    addViolation(data, assignmentExpression);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            if("String".equals(variableAccess.getType())){
                if (node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                    ASTInfixExpression expression = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);
                    if (expression.isStringAddition()) {
                        if (isInsideLoop(node)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInsideLoop(ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
        while (parent != null) {
            if (parent instanceof ASTForStatement || parent instanceof ASTWhileStatement || parent instanceof ASTDoStatement || parent instanceof ASTForeachStatement) {
                return true;
            }
            parent = parent.jjtGetParent();
        }
        return false;
    }
}

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;

```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getImage().equals("+=") && isInLoop(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInLoop(AbstractNode node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForeachStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null;
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        checkForStringAppend(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        checkForStringAppend(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkForStringAppend(Node node, Object data) {
        Node block = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if (block != null) {
            for (Node statement : block.findChildrenOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = (ASTAssignmentExpression) statement;
                if (assignmentExpression.getOperator().equals("+=")) {
                    addViolation(data, assignmentExpression);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        int count = 0;
        for(int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            if(node.jjtGetChild(i) instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = (ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetChild(i);
                if(assignmentExpression.getOperator().equals("+=")
                        && assignmentExpression.getChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression
                        && assignmentExpression.getChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    count++;
                }
            }
        }
        if(count > 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if(node.getOperator().equals("+=")
                && node.getChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression
                && node.getChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (node.getResultType().isString()) {
            checkBlock(node.getBlock(), data);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkBlock(ASTBlock block, Object data) {
        if (block == null) {
            return;
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < block.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = block.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTForeachStatement) {
                checkForeachStatement((ASTForeachStatement) child, data);
            } else if (child instanceof ASTBlock) {
                checkBlock((ASTBlock) child, data);
            }
        }
    }

    private void checkForeachStatement(ASTForeachStatement foreach, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < foreach.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = foreach.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                checkAssignmentExpression((ASTAssignmentExpression) child, data);
            } else if (child instanceof ASTBlock) {
                checkBlock((ASTBlock) child, data);
            }
        }
    }

    private void checkAssignmentExpression(ASTAssignmentExpression assignment, Object data) {
        if (assignment.jjtGetChild(0).toString().equals("description") && assignment.getOperator().equals("+=")) {
            addViolation(data, assignment);
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        int concatCount = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTBlock) {
                for (int j = 0; j < child.jjtGetNumChildren(); j++) {
                    Node subNode = child.jjtGetChild(j);
                    if (subNode instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                        Node target = subNode.jjtGetChild(0);
                        if (target.getImage() != null && target.getImage().contains("+=")) {
                            concatCount++;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        if (concatCount > 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (containsStringConcat(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean containsStringConcat(Node node) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTExpression) {
                ASTExpression expr = (ASTExpression) child;
                if (isStringConcat(expr)) {
                    return true;
                }
            }

            if (containsStringConcat(child)) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    private boolean isStringConcat(ASTExpression expr) {
        if (expr.jjtGetNumChildren() != 3 || !(expr.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator)) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentOperator op = (ASTAssignmentOperator) expr.jjtGetChild(1);
        if (!op.isCompound()) {
            return false;
        }

        return TypeHelper.isA(expr.jjtGetChild(0), String.class);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTDoStatement.class);
    }
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node childNode = node.jjtGetChild(i);
            
            if (childNode instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression assignNode = (ASTAssignmentExpression) childNode;
                if (assignNode.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTPrimaryExpression) {
                    ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpNode = (ASTPrimaryExpression) assignNode.jjtGetChild(0);
                    
                    if ("+".equals(primaryExpNode.getImage())) {
                        addViolation(data, assignNode);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);

        if (assignmentExpression != null 
            && assignmentExpression.jjtGetChild(0).getImage().contains("+")) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTDoStatement.class).stream()
            .flatMap(doStatement -> doStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentOperator.class).stream())
            .filter(ASTAssignmentOperator::isCompound)
            .forEach(op -> addViolation(data, op));

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() > 1 && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (infixExpression.getOperator().equals("+")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (isStringType(node.jjtGetChild(0)) && isStringConcatenation(node.jjtGetChild(1))) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringType(Node node) {
        return node instanceof ASTVariableAccess 
            && ((ASTVariableAccess) node).getType() == String.class;
    }

    private boolean isStringConcatenation(Node node) {
        if (node instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression expr = (ASTInfixExpression) node;
            return "+".equals(expr.getOperator())
                && (isStringType(expr.jjtGetChild(0)) || isStringType(expr.jjtGetChild(1)));
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() > 1 && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) && infixExpression.getImage().contains("+")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

    private String logStatement = "";

        for (String val : values) {

        }

        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(logStatement);
        for (String val : values) {

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.Set;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    private Set<String> vars = new HashSet<>();

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        vars.clear();
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTVariableAccess node, Object data) {
        String variableName = node.getImage();
        vars.add(variableName);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            String variableName = ((ASTVariableAccess) node.jjtGetChild(0)).getImage();
            if (vars.contains(variableName)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if(containLoop(node)) {
            super.visit(node, data);
        }

        return data;
    }

    private boolean containLoop(Node node) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);

            if (child instanceof ASTForStatement || child instanceof ASTForeachStatement || child instanceof ASTWhileStatement || child instanceof ASTDoStatement) {
                return true;
            }

            if (containLoop(child)) {
                return true;
            }
        }

        return false;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() > 1 && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);

            if (infixExpression.isConcatenation()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        Map<MethodNameDeclaration, List<NameOccurrence>> methodDeclarations = node.getScope()
                .getMethodDeclarations();

        for (Map.Entry<MethodNameDeclaration, List<NameOccurrence>> entry : methodDeclarations.entrySet()) {
            if (isMethodCalledMoreThanOnce(entry.getKey().getName(), entry.getValue())) {
                reportViolation(node, data);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isMethodCalledMoreThanOnce(String methodName, List<NameOccurrence> occurrences) {
        int count = 0;

        for (NameOccurrence occurrence : occurrences) {
            Node location = occurrence.getLocation();
            if (location instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) location;
                if (varAccess.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTInfixExpression
                        && varAccess.jjtGetParent().jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator) {
                    ASTAssignmentOperator operator = (ASTAssignmentOperator) varAccess.jjtGetParent().jjtGetChild(0);
                    if (operator.isCompound()) {
                        count++;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        return count > 1;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTExpressionStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTExpressionStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() == 1 && node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTPrimaryExpression) {
            ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression = (ASTPrimaryExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            if (primaryExpression.jjtGetNumChildren() == 3
                    && primaryExpression.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator
                    && primaryExpression.jjtGetChild(2) instanceof ASTName) {
                ASTAssignmentOperator operator = (ASTAssignmentOperator) primaryExpression.jjtGetChild(1);
                if (operator.isCompound()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super();
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
        if (parent instanceof ASTExpressionStatement) {
            Node previous = parent.jjtGetParent().jjtGetChild(parent.jjtGetIndex() - 1);
            if (previous instanceof ASTExpressionStatement) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression prevAssignment = (ASTAssignmentExpression) previous.findFirstDescendant(
                        ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
                if (prevAssignment != null && isStringAppend(prevAssignment) && isStringAppend(node)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringAppend(ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        return node.getOperator() == ASTAssignmentExpression.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN
                && node.jjtGetChild(0).getType() == String.class
                && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTStringLiteral;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.getImage().equals("+=")) {
            ASTName name = (ASTName)node.jjtGetParent().jjtGetChild(0);
            if (name.getImage().equals("String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();

        if (parent instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression && "+=".equals(parent.getImage())) {
            Node grandParent = parent.jjtGetParent();
            if (grandParent instanceof ASTVariableAccess && "String".equals(((ASTVariableAccess) grandParent).getType().getName())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        node.children().filter(ASTBlock.class::isInstance).forEach(block -> {
            int assignCount = (int) ((ASTBlock) block).children().filter(ASTForStatement.class::isInstance).flatMap(ASTForStatement::children).filter(ASTAssignmentExpression.class::isInstance).count();
            if (assignCount > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        });
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTAssignmentOperator.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentOperator node, Object data) {
        if (node.isCompound()) {
            Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
            if (parent instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression = parent.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);
                if (primaryExpression != null) {
                    ASTName name = primaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTName.class);
                    if (name != null) {
                        if (name.getImage().endsWith(".append")) {
                            return super.visit(node, data);
                        }
                    }
                }
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.Optional;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        Optional<ASTForStatement> forStatement = node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTForStatement.class)
                .stream()
                .filter(forNode -> forNode.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                        .stream()
                        .anyMatch(assignNode -> assignNode.getImage().contains("+=")))
                .findAny();

        if (forStatement.isPresent()) {
            addViolation(data, forStatement.get());
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// Test new rule example
public class Foo {
                String inefficientConcatenation() {
                    String result = "";
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        // warning: this concatenation will create one new StringBuilder per iteration
                        result += getStringFromSomeWhere(i);
                    }
                    return result;
                }

                String efficientConcatenation() {
                    // better would be to use one StringBuilder for the entire loop
                    StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        result.append(getStringFromSomeWhere(i));
                    }
                    return result.toString();
                }

                String getStringFromSomeWhere(int i) {
                    return "a" + i;
                }
            }
The description of this test case is: bad 11
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        ASTMethodDeclarator methodDeclarator = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodDeclarator.class);
        if (methodDeclarator != null && "String".equals(node.getResultType().getTypeImage())) {
            ASTBlock methodBlock = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTBlock.class);
            for (ASTBlockStatement blockStatement : methodBlock.findChildrenOfType(ASTBlockStatement.class)) {
                ASTStatement statement = blockStatement.getFirstChildOfType(ASTStatement.class);
                if (statement != null && statement.getFirstChildOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null) {
                    ASTForStatement forStatement = statement.getFirstChildOfType(ASTForStatement.class);
                    ASTStatement forBlockStatement = forStatement.getFirstChildOfType(ASTStatement.class);
                    if (forBlockStatement != null) {
                        if (forBlockStatement.jjtGetNumChildren() > 1 && forBlockStatement.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTAssignmentOperator) {
                            Node variableNode = forBlockStatement.jjtGetChild(1).jjtGetChild(0);
                            if(variableNode instanceof ASTVariableDeclaratorId && "result".equals(((ASTVariableDeclaratorId) variableNode).getImage())) {
                                addViolation(data, variableNode);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        ASTForStatement forStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTForStatement.class);
        if (forStatement != null) {
            ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = forStatement.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getImage().contains("+=")) {
                addViolation(data, assignmentExpression);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
